Important News

Jiang Bocheng, Acting Under Jiang’s Orders, Comes to Jinan 82

To Meet with Han in Weixian to Mediate the War

The Two Armies in Yexian Are at a Standstill

Jinan Correspondence: Since the outbreak of the war in eastern Shandong, people across the country have paid great attention to it during this time of national crisis. Zhang Huacun, of the Shandong Provincial Reorganization Committee, telegraphed Chiang Kai-shek in Hankou on the 20th, requesting that a senior official familiar with Shandong affairs be sent to the east to make effective mediation to avoid the suffering of the people. Chiang Kai-shek believed that Chief Counselor Jiang Bocheng had a close relationship with Han for three years, and also served as a member of the Provincial Party Department last year. He was quite familiar with the situation in Shandong, so he telegraphed Jiang, ordering him to go to Shandong to mediate as circumstances dictated. Jiang boarded a train from Ping for the south yesterday. We only received a telegram last night, and this morning (22nd) at 9 o'clock, people from all sectors of the military, government, and party went to the station to welcome him. At 9:30, Train 201 from Pingpu arrived in Jinan. Jiang got off the train and greeted the welcoming people one by one. He then went to the Jinan Central Bank to rest. I made a special trip to visit him. According to Jiang, this trip was due to an order from the Commander-in-Chief to come to Jinan to meet Chairman Han to mediate the Jiaodong Incident, hoping that both sides would first stop military action, and then deliberate on a settlement plan. Chairman Han has always been upright and has always obeyed the Commander-in-Chief, which I have always known. This action was taken as a last resort, and in the future, he will be able to obey the Commander-in-Chief's opinion to resolve the matter. Director Zhang (Xueliang) of Beiping also advocates resolving this matter as soon as possible, and also takes the Commander-in-Chief's opinion as his own. As for how to resolve it in the future, the method will be entirely decided by the central government. As for Liu Zhennian's side, I have not been in contact with him for a long time. I heard that he has reported the incident to the Commander-in-Chief. Chairman Han is currently at the front. I will accompany Committee Member Zhang Bingqian (Yue) east tonight to meet with Han to discuss everything. We plan to go to Weixian first and call Han on the phone, and then agree on a meeting place. At 5 p.m., Wang Fangting hosted a banquet for Jiang at his private residence in Zhijin City, and invited various important people to accompany him. At 12 o'clock that night, Jiang and Zhang Yue took a special train to Weixian. It is expected that they will be able to meet with Han tomorrow.

As for the situation at the front, it is reported that there is still fighting near Yexian. On the 20th, Zhang Luanji, commander of the Independent Brigade of Liu's army, led two regiments of infantry to attack Han's army from the southeast of the city. They were counterattacked head-on by Li Hanzhang's unit of the 85th Brigade of the 29th Division of Han's army. After several hours of fighting, Liu's army could not resist and retreated. At the same time, a unit of Liu's army at the Huoshen Temple in the South Gate of Yexian also bombarded Han's army with mortars. Han's army did not return fire. That afternoon, Han Fuju went to the front to inspect the front line in Shahe, arriving one mile outside the West Gate. Liu's army relied on trenches along the moat to resist the attack. There was a small conflict between the two sides, and Han immediately returned to Shahe. It is reported that three representatives of the people in Yexian City went to Han's camp in Shahe on the 21st to ask him to consider the lives of the people in the city and not to bombard the city. It is said that Liu's army in the city has begun to plunder, dismantling the doors and windows of civilian houses to repair the city moat. Civilian food has been sealed and marked, and civilians are running out of food. The morale of the army is panic-stricken. A company of garrison troops suddenly mutinied last night. Yexian has had a good autumn harvest this year, but most of the harvested crops are outside the city and have not been transported into the city. Therefore, the city is short of food and it is difficult to hold out for a long time. Han expressed that he would never use artillery bombardment unless absolutely necessary to avoid harming the people. The representatives thanked him and left. Now heavy troops and militiamen are stationed about four or five miles outside the city, like a gathering of clouds and mist, with a very strong attacking momentum, but they have not yet begun to attack. It is rumored that Liu Zhennian is also in Yexian City, but it is not known for sure. Weixian is currently rushing to build an airport for planes to take off and land. It will be completed soon (22nd).

Many Bandit Leaders in Honghu Captured 83

Hankou Correspondence: Since the bandits He and Duan fled north to Nanzhang, and the remnants of the pseudo-7th Division also fled east led by the pseudo-Division Commander Wang Yiming, there are no large gangs of red bandits in Honghu. The suppression troops there have two divisions and one independent brigade. All the important passes have been recovered one after another, and they are now searching the center of the lake. Xu Yuanquan moved from Yuekou to Xindi on the 19th to command the various units. On the 20th, he inspected the area of Xiaogangwen, Huangpeng Mountain, and Koukou, and met with Zhu Huaibing, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs that evening. They returned to Xindi together on the 21st, and went to the front line of Zhuhe again on the 22nd to supervise the army. It is reported that it has been scheduled to clear all the remaining bandits in the lake before the 25th. The war situation there has been very smooth in recent days. Xu Jiwu, the brigade commander, personally led the Niu and Ren regiments on boats into Honghu on the morning of the 18th to search for bandits. They discovered dozens of large bandit ships at Yaokou River and immediately pursued them, seizing 40 guns and capturing 16 bandits, many of whom were important bandit criminals, including Xu Caiguang, the Minister of Reorganization of the Pseudo-Xiangxiyu Military Committee, Wu Chunfang, the Minister of Organization of the Pseudo-Xiang'exi-Hubei-Shaanxi Provincial Federation of Trade Unions, Sun Huatang, the Chief of Staff of the Pseudo-Education Army and the current Chief of the Intelligence Section of the Pseudo-Xiang'exi Provincial Military Committee, Zhou Shaolou, the manager of the Pseudo-3rd Army, and Chen Wenjin, the director of the Financial Department of the Pseudo-7th Division. They have all been sent to Xindi to await interrogation. In Shijagou, Xiaotasi, and other places, more than 300 bandit soldiers were found, but they were all scarred and starving to death. They were also escorted to Xindi by the brigade to await orders. It is particularly noteworthy that the bandits value guns and ammunition very much. They do not fire a single bullet during the exchange of fire, and even if they are defeated, they would rather sacrifice more people than abandon a gun, because all sides are blocked and there is no way to get supplies. Since the 10th Army entered the lake, they have seized a large number of bandit guns, and they are still engaged in searching for guns. The 41st Division seized 66 rifles in Tongzi Lake on the 17th, 139 rifles on the 18th, and 8 mortars and 46 rifles south of Tongzi Lake on the 19th. A large number of weapons were also seized in Xihugang, Taxiehe, Chenjiadun, Datokou, Jiangsikou, Zhengdaohu, and Sunjiatai. On the 20th, the division continued to seize 26 rifles and carbines, 1 submachine gun and 1 pistol, 5 or 6 major pieces of machinery from the arsenal, 17 small pieces of machinery, and more than 120 parts. On the 21st, 81 rifles and carbines were seized in Potian Goufangjiawan, Li Haichun, a pseudo-battalion commander, was captured, and a large part of the arsenal's machinery and a radio were salvaged. Xu Jiwu Brigade of the 48th Division seized 11 mortars, 21 gun carriages, and 77 rifles. Xue's Regiment of the New 3rd Brigade also found more than 300 rifles stored by the bandits south of Dukou Dakou. It can be seen that the red bandits there are now only concerned with escaping, and they do not care about the guns. Commander Chiang Kai-shek telegraphed Xu Yuanquan to convey his praise for the loyalty and courage of Zhang and Liu's units in striking at the bandit dens. He also telegraphed Zeng Yiding, the commander of the Second Fleet of the Navy, to convey his praise for the meritorious service of the Yong Sui, Min Sheng, Min Quan, Xian Ning, De Sheng, Wei Sheng, Shun Sheng, Gong Sheng, Yi Sheng, and Ren Sheng warships in patrolling the upper reaches of the Yangtze River and assisting in the suppression, in order to encourage them (September 23rd).

Jiang Guangding and Cai Tingkai Arrive in Fujian 84

Jiang and Cai Go to Zhangzhou Upon Arrival in Xiamen

Jiang Then Goes to the Provincial Capital from Zhangzhou

Situation in Xiamen: Xiamen Correspondence: Jiang Guangding, Director of the Fujian Pacification Office, and Cai Tingkai, Commander of the 19th Route Army, arrived in Xiamen on the Java Company's Zhi Ni Jianana輪 on the afternoon of the 16th. After lunch, they went to Songyu by electric boat with Jiang Yanfu, Lin Yuheng, Xu Minghong, Tang Dehuang, and others who came with them. When Jiang and others arrived in Xiamen, Lin Guogeng, Commander of the Zhangzhou and Xiamen Garrison, Huang Qiang, Chief of Staff of the 19th Route Army, Zhang Yan, Deputy Commander of the 61st Division, Zhang Li, Commander of the 121st Brigade, Zhou Xingnan, Director of the 19th Route Army Office, Yang Shaotang, Deputy Director, and more than 30 others all came to welcome them. Jiang gave a speech to the press on the ship. (Reporter asked) The Fujian Provincial Defense Army has always been criticized by the public, and has recently had conflicts with the people from time to time. I don’t know if it will still be under the command of the provincial government in the future. Director Jiang must have a plan in mind. Can you tell us about it? (Jiang replied) This matter has not been discussed yet, and I cannot express it at this time. (Asked) He Xianzhu, the deputy commander of the 3rd Mixed Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army, recently extorted tobacco seedling donations and sent troops to massacre Dongsha Village. It is said that the clan chief of the village and people from Putian and Xianyou have sent telegrams to the Pacification Office to accuse He. How will Director Jiang deal with this matter? (Answered) I don’t know the situation of this matter, and I haven’t received a report. (Asked) Regarding the military affairs of suppressing the Communists in western Fujian, will Commander Cai still be in charge in the future? (Answered) Commander Cai will still be in charge. (Asked) When will Director Jiang go to the province? (Answered) In a day or two. (Asked) Will the Director go ashore today or go directly to Zhangzhou? (Answered) Go ashore first, and then go to Zhangzhou after resting. Lin Guogeng and Cai Tingkai had already approached at this point, and Jiang and Lin and others went to the Ping Dian Lun of the Bank of China and landed at the Zhangfu Wharf. It was exactly 12:40 p.m. The Maritime Public Security Bureau sent Inspector Liao Weijin to lead more than a dozen water police officers to take the electric boat to protect them. The Marine Corps Company of the 19th Route Army was dispatched on shore to post sentries, and the detective team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau also arrived. After Jiang, Cai, Lin, and others landed, they went to the fourth floor of the 19th Route Army Office to rest, talked for about 20 minutes, and Lin Guogeng resigned and returned to the headquarters. Jiang and others had lunch at the office. At 2:30 p.m., Jiang, Cai, Huang Qiang, Tang Dehuang, Jiang Yanfu, and others took the electric boat of the Road Administration Office to Songyu and entered Zhangzhou. At the same time, the Maritime Public Security Bureau also sent 12 armed water police officers to take the Zhonghe electric boat to escort them to Song. The 19th Route Army Headquarters in Zhangzhou sent a squad of guards to escort them on the Daban Sheng electric boat.

Situation in the Province: Fuzhou Correspondence: After Jiang Guangding and Cai Tingkai entered Zhangzhou from Xiamen, Jiang returned to Xiamen from Zhangzhou. On the 19th, he took the Hai Teng Xialun from Xiamen again and arrived at Luoxing Pagoda in Majiang at 11:30 on the morning of the 20th with Deng Shizeng, Chief of Staff of the Pacification Office, and Chen Weiyuan, representative of Fang Shengtao. He rested briefly at the Naval Entertainment Club. Those who came to Majiang to welcome them that day included Xing Dian, Director of the Adjutant's Office, Fan Zongchi, Director of the General Staff Office, Tan Qixiu, Brigade Commander, members of the provincial government, the deputy commander of the martial law, and the brigade commander of the 1st Brigade of the Army. Before long, Jiang and others left the Lianhuan Club and took a fast boat to the province. Fang, the acting chairman of the Taijiang Naval Public Office, and the heads of the Ministry of Civil Affairs, Finance and Education, as well as all the commissioners of the Provincial Party Department, were waiting there. Representatives of various social organizations also went to the new Taijiang Wharf or Wanshou Bridge to express their welcome. After Jiang shook hands with Fang as a courtesy, Fang invited him to board a car and go to the city to go directly to the Pacification Office. The sound of firecrackers was loud along the way. After Jiang arrived at the Pacification Office, he personally came out to meet the representatives of various social organizations and thanked them for their welcome. The representatives of the social organizations also gave welcome speeches and expressed their expectations for the two matters of suppressing the Communists and resisting Japan. After that, Jiang went to the provincial government to visit Fang, the acting chairman, and then returned to his residence to rest (September 21st).

Important News 2 85

After the Recovery of Jinjiazhai in Xinji, It is Decided to Establish Jingfu and Lihuang Counties 86

A New Military Agricultural System Will Be Piloted

Uncultivated Land Will Be Given to Soldiers to Cultivate

A dispatch from Hankou reports that Xinji, belonging to Guangshan County in Henan Province, and Jinjiazhai, belonging to Lu'an County in Anhui Province, have been bandit dens for several years. Xinji was the location of the puppet "Henan-Hubei-Anhui Three-Province Soviet," gathering a large number of bandits. Jinjiazhai was particularly famous for its rugged mountain roads and precipitous terrain. For nearly a hundred years since the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom, it has long been a haven for bandits, even called "the modern Liangshan Marsh." The Red bandits have occupied this place for six years. Their leaders are Kuang Jixun, Xu Xiangqian, Liao Chakun, Zhang Guotao, Chen Changhao, Xu Bingzhong, Deng Zhigao, etc., possessing tens of thousands of troops. They take Xinji, Jinjiazhai, Qiliping, Xuanhuadian, Shangcheng, Yingshan, Huang'an, and Zhufo'an as their military and political center, making every effort to operate. In Xinji and Jinjiazhai, they have built extremely solid fortifications, stockpiling grain and ammunition, believing that they can take the three provinces if they advance, and defend themselves if they retreat. Recently, the government army advanced in multiple routes, winning victories one after another. All important towns have been recovered in order. Jinjiazhai was the last to fall, and the remnant bandits fled in disorder. Although they have not been completely wiped out, their base area is completely lost. The time for complete suppression should not be far off. Commander-in-chief Chiang Kai-shek believes that Xinji is located between Bopi River in Guangshan County, Henan Province, and Qiliping in Huang'an County, Hubei Province, and has been deeply influenced by bandits. Jinjiazhai is more than 200 li away from Lu'an County, more than 200 li away from Huoqiu County, and more than 100 li away from Shangcheng County in Henan Province. For the sake of permanent peace and convenience of control, it is necessary to change the county governance. It was originally planned to rename Xinji as Yongjing County and Jinjiazhai as Yongning County. Later, because Liu Zhi and Wei Lihuang made great contributions to suppressing bandits, it was decided to rename Xinji as Jingfu County and Jinjiazhai as Lihuang County to commemorate their achievements. Both are under the jurisdiction of Henan Province. The county magistrate is also recommended by Liu Zhi. Although his duty is that of a county magistrate, he is actually treated as an administrative inspector commissioner, increasing his status and giving him power, so that he can be responsible for handling local affairs. It is heard that Liu has selected two capable officers and recommended them to Chiang, and detailed the local disaster situation, requesting emergency relief. Chiang has replied by telegram asking Liu to plan and decide to do his best to remedy the situation. The land problem in the bandit area should also be solved. According to a staff member of the headquarters, wherever the Red bandits have occupied for a long time, they have implemented the slogan of "overthrowing local tyrants and distributing land." In reality, only the real Red Army enjoyed the distribution of land. Also, because they were plundering everywhere, they could not cultivate and harvest. The real farmers were driven to become "substitute cultivation teams." As a result, "substitute cultivation" became "lazy cultivation." Therefore, the so-called Red areas were nothing but barren and desolate land. Now, the headquarters has invited experts to discuss and has drafted regulations on military agricultural settlements in the bandit areas, stipulating that if the area of abandoned land in each county in the bandit areas exceeds six-tenths of the total cultivated land in the county, it will be designated as a military agricultural settlement county. All abandoned land in the military agricultural settlement county will be confiscated and owned by the public, and land will be distributed to the active soldiers for cultivation according to the number of people. Approximately three to seven mu of land will be allocated to each soldier. All detailed regulations will be announced soon. This military agricultural settlement method will be first piloted in Jingfu and Lihuang counties. (September 23)

The Legislative Yuan Passes the Hubei Provincial Public Bond Ordinance 87

The Hubei Provincial Government, due to the urgent need for funds for bandit suppression in Hubei Province, specially requested the Executive Yuan to approve the issuance of 3 million yuan of short-term public bonds for Hubei Province for post-war recovery to meet the need. The Executive Yuan forwarded it to the Ministry of Finance for review. The Ministry of Finance believed that Hubei Province needed funds for bandit suppression, which was a real situation, and the request could be approved. It was then presented to the Executive Yuan, which was submitted to the Central Political Conference. The 324th meeting on the 22nd resolved to approve the issuance and submit it to the Legislative Yuan for review according to law. On the morning of the 24th, the 203rd regular meeting of the Legislative Yuan was submitted for discussion and resolved to amend and pass it. The public bond regulations are recorded as follows: (Article 1) The Hubei Provincial Government, for the purpose of handling pacification and post-war recovery, specially issues public bonds, named the Hubei Provincial Post-War Recovery Public Bonds of the Republic of China in 1932. (Article 2) The fixed amount of this public bond is 3 million national currency. (Article 3) The annual interest rate of this public bond is set at 8%. (Article 4) This public bond will be issued on October 1, 1932. (Article 5) The interest payment date for this public bond will be June 30 and December 31 of each year, starting from October 1932. (Article 6) December 31, 1933, is the date for the first redemption of this public bond. After that, the principal will be redeemed every six months, with an average redemption of one-twelfth, and 500,000 yuan will be redeemed each year until the end of June 1939. The redemption of bond tickets will be determined by lottery. The aforementioned lottery will be conducted by the Finance Department at the location of the provincial government on June 15 and December 15 of each year. Representatives will be sent by the provincial government and auditing agencies, and representatives will be sent by the Hankou and Wuchang Chambers of Commerce to supervise together. (Article 7) The principal and interest payment of this public bond will be funded by the provincial business tax revenue. The amount listed in the principal and interest repayment schedule will be deposited in the designated bank each time for special storage, ready for payment of principal and interest upon maturity. (Article 8) After the issuance of this public bond, the provincial government will organize a fund management committee to be responsible for the custody of the public bond fund and supervise the principal and interest payment. The aforementioned fund management committee will be organized by one person each from the provincial government, the finance department, the civil affairs department, the auditing agency, and the Hankou municipal government, and one representative each from the Hankou, Wuchang, and Hanyang Chambers of Commerce, and the Hankou Bank and Money Industry Associations. (Article 9) The bond tickets for this public bond are divided into four types: 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, 10 yuan, and 5 yuan, all of which are unregistered. (Article 10) This public bond may be freely bought and sold or mortgaged. When it is necessary to pay a deposit for other provincial official duties, it may be used as collateral. (Article 11) Those who forge this public bond or damage its credit will be punished by the judicial organs according to law. (Article 12) The rules for the issuance of this public bond and the regulations of the fund management committee shall be determined by the Hubei Provincial Government. (Article 13) This ordinance shall come into effect on the date of promulgation.

Record of a Journey West (II) (X) (VII) 88

Our whole group has decided to set off for Yichuan in three days. I heard that this trip will involve climbing over three big mountains, so everyone can't help but feel a little scared. According to the information gathered from local travelers over the past few days regarding the route from Yan'an back to Xi'an, it is roughly as follows:

(1) From Yan'an to Yichuan, you pass through 30 li of mountain road to Angou, 30 li of flat road to Aqingzhai, 10 li of flat road to Donghunerwan, 10 li of flat road to Pitou Village, 30 li of downhill road to Yunyan, 10 li of flat road to Guanyigou, 10 li of uphill road to Dingjia Yaogou, 30 li of flat road to Jiaoli, and another 30 li of uphill road to Yichuan, for a total of 180 li.

(2) From Yichuan to Hukou, there are only 50 li of small mountain roads, for a round trip of 100 li.

(3) From Yichuan to Jiyi Town, you pass through 10 li of flat road to Guo Jiawan, 40 li of mountain road to Xuejiaping, and 50 li of mountain gully road to Jiyi Town, for a total of 100 li.

(4) From Jiyi to Longmen, you pass through 30 li of mountain road to Tujuan Village, 30 li of mountain road to Niuwang Temple, 10 li of gully road to Ya Cha, and 30 li of mountain road to Longmen, for a total of 90 li.

(5) From Longmen to Hancheng, you pass through 30 li of flat road to Zhan Village, and another 30 li of flat road to Hancheng, for a total of 60 li.

(6) From Hancheng to Taiyang, there are 90 li of motor road.

(7) From Taiyang to Dali, there are 115 li of motor road.

(8) From Dali to Sanyuan and Xi'an, you can take a car.

People and Horses Exhausted Arrive at Yunyan 89

Although the oil of Yanchang is the only product that makes Yanchang increase its status, after three days, we were already satiated with the smell of oil, and finally had to leave reluctantly. I remember that day was September 3rd. Because of the lack of a good horse, I had to change to a small donkey. It didn't walk very fast. I sat on its back and had plenty of time to browse all the natural beauty. The clear spring in the stream seemed to be playing a constant rhythm. The pearl dew on the green grass was inadvertently destroyed by the trampling of the donkey's hooves. If the dew knew, it would definitely scold the imperialist behavior of mankind. After an hour or two, we parted with the stream and walked into the mountains. At first, the weak donkey seemed to be able to勉强 follow the horses. However, the mountain became steep, and it was too weak to climb the mountain, so I had to come down and lead it straight up the green mountain path. After a few minutes, the horse tracks in front of me became blurred and even disappeared. Alas, I had fallen behind. When I reached the high mountain plain, although I鞭驴疾走, I could not see the riders in front, nor the people sitting on the luggage mules behind. I was like Zhang Guolao riding a donkey alone, in the vast mountains, there was a possibility of getting lost everywhere. My heart was very full. For a moment, I felt that the beautiful little flowers on the side of the road seemed to be義誚ing the uneducated traveler. The wheat ears in the field, which were raised and had not yet垂垂, laughed very傲慢ly at the monotonous行人. The clouds passed slowly, and the wind came萧萧. It did not give any guidance to my future. In the crossroads where people徘徊摸索, the wind and clouds, which are the most out of all material things, seemed to be pulling their faces and becoming snobbish. I finally arrived at Aqingzhai, the place where all the 打煎 was located, at one o'clock in the afternoon, and met with the riders. We sat on the stones in twos and threes to rest. After half an hour, we saw the luggage mule team coming湾湾曲曲游蜓 like a long snake. At that time, our only lunch, noodles and 玉蜀黍, had already been cooked in the home of an old 百姓, waiting for the cook to bring them out. The pressure on our stomachs was too利害, so we devoured them like狼吞虎嚥. We had all given up all unnatural虚伪, and unintentionally暴露着 mankind's固有的天真 in Shaanxi from time to time, just like the巍大的山脉 exposed the coal oil or other treasures that he had蕴积 for thousands of years. (To be continued)

Songjiang 90

Minutes of the Red Branch Meeting: The Songjiang Red Branch held its sixth meeting at the meeting hall on Malu Bridge on the afternoon of the 22nd of this month. Chairman Sheng Yuanyin's agenda included: (1) Whether the epidemic hospital should be closed early. Resolved: Because the weather is getting colder and the epidemic atmosphere has been killed, and all the inpatients have been cured and discharged, and because the funds of this branch are extremely short due to not issuing donation booklets, it is decided to close it early at the end of this month to save expenses. (2) Reassignment of the staff of the office of this branch. Resolved: Wu Chengfu is promoted to executive director and Zhu Zishou is promoted to secretary and designer. In addition to sending letters urging them to take office on a specific date, Huang Xiaohe is also promoted to assist in the work to facilitate the progress. (3) The case of purchasing a base for the construction of the meeting hall of this branch. Resolved: Promote Du Ruozhou, Qu Zhiliang, Bai Guan, and Hong Tong to design and negotiate to purchase a base first, so as to raise funds for construction and preserve it for a long time. (4) How to make up for the insufficient funds of the current epidemic hospital. Resolved: It is estimated that there will be a shortfall of more than 1,000 yuan at the end of this session, which will be raised by members and staff to make up for it. (5) Adding members to the asset committee. Resolved: Add Zhu Guanghan, Zheng Hanqing, and Yang Boliang as members of the asset committee of this branch. The meeting adjourned after the agenda was completed.

Merchants Request Postponement of Implementation of Weights and Measures: The county government was ordered to promote weights and measures, and first sent personnel to inspect the scales and rulers of various industries on a daily basis. Now, various trade associations feel that it is inconvenient to gather and change to the new system. Yesterday, a joint meeting was convened at the county chamber of commerce to report that the old scales of the copper, tin, iron, lacquer, candle, and flour industries that have been investigated have been sealed and canceled. It is ordered to change to the new system of weights and measures within one week. If the old instruments are still used during the second phase of the investigation, they will be detained and punished. However, Suzhou, which was the old provincial capital and a place with flourishing commerce, has not yet heard of the implementation of the new system of weights and measures. Shanghai, which is the gathering place of national commerce, has once investigated weights and measures, but it has been several months and there is no news of changing to the new system. The source of commercial goods in Song City mostly comes from Suzhou and Shanghai. If Songyi changes to the new system before Suzhou and Shanghai, Song merchants will suffer losses and it is unbearable. After discussion by the crowd, it was generally agreed that it would be appropriate to wait until Suzhou and Shanghai implement the new system before Songyi follows suit. The decision was telegraphed to the provincial government, requesting that the county be ordered to postpone the implementation temporarily to alleviate the difficulties of merchants.

The County Chamber of Commerce Re-elects Chairman: After the death of the former chairman of the County Chamber of Commerce, Chen Ru, Liu Zhuren was补选 as chairman. Later, members such as Chen Shushu filed a complaint with the Department of Industry, accusing Liu Zhuren of illegal 补选, and stating that five people including Zhixing Fang Lunyuan had lost their membership status. Nantong 97

Naval Fleet Concentrates in Tong: The warships of the first fleet of the Navy were ordered to concentrate on the river surface of Nantong Lujing Port. On the 24th, Commander Chen Jiliang led the fleet to the waters outside Xiangshan Port for joint exercises.

Change of Battalion Commander of the Customs Police Camp Stationed in Tong: Yi Ziqi, the battalion commander of the third battalion of the Customs Police stationed in Tong under the Ministry of Finance, was dismissed by order of the commander-in-chief Mo Xiong, and Ge Nanshan was appointed to replace him. The handover took place on the 23rd.

Deadline for Payment of Jingwu Road款: The Provincial Government telegraphed the County Government, setting the deadline for the remittance of the allocated Jingwu Road款 for a thorough settlement before the 25th.

Jiading 98

Cotton Harvest is Hopeless: Due to the arid weather during the growing season of the cotton in the county, the cotton failed to develop well. Now, when it is time to实绽吐絮, there has been continuous阴雨, which has caused most of the结棉桃 to rot. Although the weather has cleared up today, the bleak situation has been set. At most, there will only be three or four成收成. After years of drought and disaster and having suffered寇患, now that the cotton harvest is hopeless, all sectors are worrying.

Slaughter Tax Reduced Again and Again for Bidding: Feng Kaisheng, the slaughter tax collector of the county, resigned after the兵燹. The Provincial Education Fund Management Office then entrusted the County Government to invite bids for contracting. The first bid amount was 9,000 yuan, and the bidding was opened on August 15. The second bid amount was 8,500 yuan, and the bidding was opened on September 10. Neither resulted in anyone submitting a bid. Now, the amount has been reduced again to 8,000 yuan for the third invitation to bid, which is scheduled to be opened on September 29.

Rugao 99

Preventing Immense Calamities Caused by Welcoming Gods and Holding Temple Fairs On the 18th of this month in the morning, the local populace suddenly spread the word that the Wu Xiang Temple was about to welcome gods and hold temple fairs. Upon hearing the news, various organizations immediately convened a meeting to discuss methods of prevention. It was agreed that a letter would be sent to the Third Company of the Provincial Security Force stationed in Pu Province, requesting them to dispatch 40 men. The Protection Corps would dispatch 7 men, and the Public Security Bureau would dispatch 10 men to go and peacefully persuade them to desist. At 5:00 AM on the 19th, various organizations arrived at the temple and saw over two hundred men and women burning incense, gathered in front of the temple gate, showing no signs of disturbance. Unexpectedly, in less than an hour, the sound of gongs arose from all directions, and in an instant, a crowd of one or two thousand people gathered, surrounding the Wu Xiang Temple, throwing incense fiercely into the temple. The crowd grew larger and larger. The Provincial Security Force and others inside tried to persuade them with great effort but to no avail. It was said that gunshots were heard in the midst of the crowd. Seeing this situation, the police and security forces were deeply concerned that bandits might be hiding among them, taking the opportunity to riot, so they fired shots into the sky as a warning and retreated from the temple gate. The Director and Company Commander were both beaten and injured. Police officers from the Provincial Security Force, the Protection Corps, and the Public Security Bureau were tied up with cloth by the rioters and placed behind the temple, where they were burned. They were later sent to the hospital for treatment. The police and security forces lost five rifles. Among the populace, three male and one female villager were found dead from gunshot wounds. Upon receiving the news, the county government immediately dispatched the third squad leader of the county police to suppress the situation. The county government also ordered the arrest of Wu Chen and Long Hua, the monks of the Wu Xiang Temple, as well as the village head and the police officer involved in the incident, and brought them to the government office for interrogation.

Liuhe 100

The Seventh District Chief Accused The Seventh District Chief, Dong Qinghan, is accused of corruption and dereliction of duty in the Zhu Town area. The people of the district have repeatedly filed complaints. It is now known that the Department of Civil Affairs has ordered County Magistrate Chen Bingbo to conduct an impartial investigation and report the findings for review. Furthermore, the Eighth District Chief, He Wenjian, is said to be detained by the county government for failing to account for public funds and being in arrears.

Hangzhou 101

Public Burial of Aviation Martyr Shi Manniu The training aircraft No. 852 of the Hangzhou Jianqiao Aviation School crashed during a test flight. Instructor Shi Manniu and Chen Ying's eldest son, Chen Shenfu, were killed in the crash. Chen's coffin had already been transported back to his hometown by his family. Shi Manniu's remains were still placed in the Caishen Temple in Jianqiao. Now that Shi's elderly mother, Madam Shi Chen, heard the tragic news of Shi's death, she attempted suicide several times in Zhengzhou. Fortunately, her eldest son, Zifeng, persuaded her with all his might, and she traveled to Hangzhou with her eldest daughter-in-law to mourn at the coffin. The second son, Ziyun, who usually traded in Shanghai, had gone to Hanzhou to collect debts when the accident occurred and also rushed to the scene. The Principal of the Aviation School, Mao Bangchu, and his wife, as well as the Provincial Chairman, Guan Diping, and others, personally went to express their condolences. The Aviation School, in memory of the martyrs who sacrificed their lives for aviation, purchased over ten acres of land ten miles from Jianqiao to build a public cemetery for aviation martyrs. Shi's remains will be buried there first. The school is now planning to hold a grand memorial service around Double Ten Day to express their grief.

Ningbo 102

Bandits Burn Ancestral Hall Houses Near Lantian Dongjiaqiao, in the deep mountains bordering Fengnan and Songlin, Ninghai County, banditry has been rampant recently. Some days ago, at noon, 120 soldiers were having lunch in an ancestral hall in the village when bandits learned of it. They assumed that the villagers had specially sent soldiers to arrest them. After the soldiers left, they burned the entire ancestral hall to the ground. The residents are now in a state of panic. Ouyang Ge Inspects Two Ships Ouyang Ge, Director of the Offshore Water Police Bureau, along with Inspector Yang Lin, Chief of the First Section Xie Zezhi, and others, went to the Chao Wu and Hai Jing ships, which were docked in the Zhenhai River, for an inspection to understand the strength of the water police. Finally, they also inspected the land patrol team. It lasted for four hours before they returned to the bureau.

Xiaoshan 103

Police Force and Protection Corps Jointly Suppress Bandits The Tianle, Shimen, and Huang areas in the southern part of Xiaoshan have always been bandit dens. The kidnapping of children from residents outside the southeast gate of Xiaoshan was carried out by bandits from that area. The governments of Shaoxing and Xiaoshan counties ordered the Seventh Public Security Bureau and the entire Protection Corps to launch a joint suppression to pacify the area.

Large Swarms of Locusts Pass Through On the 19th and 20th, large swarms of locusts suddenly passed through the sandy lands of Dongsha, Yujiatan, Tangcun, and Fengshui in Xiaoshan County, flying from the northwest to the southeast. All the green bamboo canopies and sand grasses were eaten. The sand dwellers are now trying to exterminate them.

The Fourth Meeting of the Zhongda Screening Committee 104

Nanjing, 24th Telegram The Central Screening Examination Committee held its fourth meeting on the 24th and resolved: (1) Yang Shangpu, a student who returned from studying in Japan, applied to audit classes but did not attend the school. The application was approved. (2) Regarding the transfer cases, it was decided that approval would not be granted. (3) Huang Qin Xuan and two other auditors from Chengdu University requested to be changed to regular students. It was decided that approval would not be granted. (4) Wu Di and other auditors from China Public School requested to continue auditing classes. It was decided that approval would not be granted. (5) Regarding the passing standard for the screening examination results, it was decided that students who pass the screening examination with a passing overall average score and a passing score in each subject are considered passing. Those who fail the overall average score, or those who pass the overall average score but fail three subjects, are considered failing and will be demoted by one grade. Those who have no grade to be demoted to will be ordered to take a leave of absence.

Shanghai International Robert Cup Maintained by China for Three Consecutive Years 115

Yesterday, Lin and Qiu Defeated British De Fufu and White 3-1

Sun Linfang Defeated Sun Na to Win the Shanghai Junior Singles Championship

Yesterday, Chinese Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai defeated British De Fufu and White with full spirit and after four sets of fierce battle, winning the Robert Cup for the third consecutive year. More than a thousand spectators rejoiced in the success of Lin and Qiu in winning glory for the Chinese tennis world, in addition to enjoying the feast for the eyes. In the Junior Singles Final, Sun Linfang also defeated Sun Na 3-1 to win the championship. The Junior Singles competition has been won by China every year since 1930, for three years now. The first time was Yu Tianguang, the second time was Qian Wenbao, and this year, yesterday, was the third time for Sun Linfang. It cannot be said that the progress of the Chinese tennis world in recent years is not significant. Yesterday's matches were held at the French Chamber of Commerce. The details are recorded below:

Junior Singles 116

|Sun Linfang Wins the Championship|

Starting at 2:15 PM, Sun Linfang and Sun Na began competing for the Junior Singles Championship. The performance of the two was mediocre and lacked excitement. Because their techniques lacked both variety and skill, it was boring. In the first set, Sun Linfang showed timidity everywhere. He was unable to calmly deal with the opponent's mediocre shots and often made unforced errors. As a result, Sun lost the first set 2-6. Sun showed some improvement in the second set, and the opponent repeatedly lost points. Sun won 6-3. In the third set, Sun Na was at a loss, while Sun's spirit gradually recovered. The timidity was somewhat removed, and he won 6-1 without much effort. The competition in the fourth set was more intense, and the situation was quite tense. However, Sun could have won but was careless. In a mediocre situation, he caused the audience to worry about Sun's gains and losses. From 2-2, 3-3, all the way to 6-6, 7-7, Sun had the advantage at times, but unexpectedly, this situation developed. Fortunately, he added two more games at the end and won the final victory 9-7.

Robert Cup 117

|China Wins the Championship|

Brief Description of Skills Yesterday, the cooperation between Lin and Qiu was flawless. There was no significant difference in the individual skills of the two. They both performed well. Qiu Feihai maintained a calm attitude throughout. Lin Shihua still inevitably made one or two mistakes in his high-pressure shots, which he has always regarded as difficult, but his successful

Robert Cup China-England Final (Yongfang Photography) 118

works cannot be said to be few. His forehand strokes also had few mistakes. His serve was his specialty, and he used it to score points. In short, the two were in high spirits and worked hard, causing the famous generals De Fufu and White to admit defeat. As for England's defeat, it was due to White's inability to replicate his usual performance. He often disappointed. De Fufu was as strong as ever and had brilliant moments. His performance was no less than Lin and Qiu's.

Winning Two Sets in a Row The match followed the conclusion of the Junior Singles Final. De Fufu failed to serve, and Lin Baohua won the serve. China then won two games. Later, White and Qiu took turns serving, each winning one game. England's momentum suddenly became strong. Lin and Qiu's high balls were improperly returned, giving the opponent a chance to intercept. England took a 5-3 lead. China was in immediate danger. Fortunately, De Fufu's serve failed, and Lin Baohua's serve won, turning the tide and making it 5-5. After that, England took the lead at times, and Lin and Qiu equalized. After 7-7, China added two more games in a row and reversed the defeat with a score of 9-7. From the second set onwards, China progressed smoothly. The ball was often aimed at both sides, making it difficult for the enemy to parry. Lin Baohua's serve often won. As a result, they won 6-3. The competition in the last game was particularly fierce, with five ties. Whether it was a volley, a high ball, or a high-pressure shot, each side displayed their strengths in a variety of ways. However, De Fufu's serve had three double faults, which led to Lin and Qiu's victory.

One Gain and One Loss In the first two sets, Lin and Qiu were in high spirits, doing whatever they wanted and succeeding easily. They thought it would be easy to win three straight sets, but unexpectedly, Lin and Qiu changed their previous state in the third set, feeling dull and getting worse and worse. They lost 1-6, so they continued to work hard in the competition in the fourth set, making four games in one go. However, Lin Baohua's serve in the following game ended in a disastrous defeat. In De Fufu's serve, Lin and Qiu often sent high balls, but they were too close to the net, giving the opponent a chance to attack, resulting in a 4-3 score, and then 4-4. The situation suddenly became equal again. Lin and Qiu won back one game of White's serve and regained priority. The next game was Lin's serve. The audience clapped their hands to welcome it, wishing him success. Sure enough, he lived up to expectations and won the championship with a score of 6-4.

Local News

National League Conference Reported by Wireless Telephone 126

First Broadcast from the 26th of This Month

Shanghai Residents Can Hear the Voice of the World Peace Envoy

The current session of the League of Nations in Geneva is of utmost importance to the continued existence of human peace and the extension of world justice. To our country, because of the tense Sino-Japanese negotiations, the stakes are even higher. Special attention should be paid to the situation of the meeting. According to the League of Nations' own radio station, it has been in direct 24-hour communication with our local international radio station. The information is very fast. In order to widely publicize its work, the League of Nations has specifically set Greenwich Mean Time, broadcasting important work news every Sunday at 10 pm via wireless telephone. This corresponds to 6:00 am to 6:15 am every Monday morning in Shanghai time, broadcasting in French. From 6:15 am to 6:30 am, broadcasting in English, and from 6:30 am to 6:45 am, broadcasting in Spanish. The wavelengths are 20.64 and 40.3 meters. Previously, it had been in contact with the local international radio station for testing. The sound waves are exceptionally clear. Tomorrow (the 26th) at 6:00 am, the first broadcast will be held, with Mr. Drummond, Secretary-General of the League of Nations, personally delivering a speech. Those in this city who have radios can pay special attention to listening at that time to hear the voice of the world peace envoy.

Liaohai Customs to be Blockaded Starting Today 127

Tax Collection Methods Announced Yesterday

Regarding the blockade of the Northeast Customs, after Finance Minister Song officially issued a declaration, it will be implemented starting today. Although the authorities announced the method of tax collection in a different place after the implementation of the blockade yesterday, after the customs received this instruction yesterday, due to the urgency of time, the published text had slight discrepancies in wording and was not easy for people to understand. Shanghai United National Shipping Alliance 130

Regulating Business

Maintaining Navigation Rights

Already in Preparation

Among the Chinese shipping companies, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Sanpei Steam Navigation Company, and Ning Shao Steam Navigation Company have been the largest in scale and business. In recent years, small-scale shipping companies have gradually increased in the Yangtze River and coastal routes, numbering about 40. They all have irregular routes and infrequent schedules, loading and transporting passengers and goods anytime and anywhere. The "January 28th Incident" occurred this year, and silver money companies have been cautious in lending money. Various trade guilds have reduced their purchases, and the shipping industry has been most affected. In addition, the Northeast was forcibly occupied by Japan, navigation rights were lost, national ships cannot travel smoothly, and the scope of shipping is further reduced. Chinese shipping is in danger of collapsing. Chen Bogang and Yu Qiaqing, chairmen of the Shanghai Shipping Association, in order to save national ships and maintain navigation rights, implemented a United National Shipping Alliance to resist the encroachment of foreign ships. The reporter heard the news and went to various parties for detailed investigations and reports the general situation as follows:

Reasons for the Alliance: There are more than 40 Chinese shipping companies of all sizes in Shanghai. Except for a few with fixed routes and schedules, the rest are small in scale, with only one or two merchant ships and no fixed routes. Most of them dispatch ships temporarily to load and transport passengers and goods. There are often several ships competing to sail to one place, and they abuse fare reductions in order to compete for cargo, disrupting business and destroying freight rates. This year, there is a shortage of goods in various places, and shipping has plummeted. Among the dozens of national ships in Shanghai, only the China Wei and Da Tong companies have better business. Since the puppet state and Japan signed a treaty, the routes of national ships have become more restricted. Chen Bogang and Yu Qiaqing, chairmen of the Shanghai Shipping Association, agreed to save the sluggish Chinese shipping industry and decided to start with the alliance of the whole body of companies to cooperate.

Methods of Unity: Chen and Yu proposed the united national ships, advocating open business and avoiding fierce competition. Chen has presented this theme to all members, and all companies have expressed their sympathy. The general method of this unity is to unite all shipping companies and allocate all merchant ships according to the original routes of each ship, then jointly controlled by the joint office, so as to ensure an average, to adjust excesses and deficiencies, so that freight rates are uniform, and no unauthorized increases or decreases are allowed. Its business is handled in accordance with the Lian'an Shipping Bureau method of the six companies on the Shanghai-Taiwan line, so as to maintain long-term operations.

Maintaining Navigation Rights: After the establishment of the United National Shipping Alliance, it can eliminate internal competition among the same industry, freight and passenger fares will also be unified, schedules will be fixed, and there will be no worry about the lack of ships or goods. It is also more convenient for passengers, and the ships can be used to control the traffic on the Yangtze River and coastal routes to prevent foreign merchants' ships from coveting and encroaching. National goods in various ports that resist enemy ships can be transported by national ships. This move is also of great significance for maintaining navigation rights. This matter is currently being planned and managed by Mr. Chen and will be completed soon.

Freight Rate Issue: Regarding the issue of freight rates and cash payments, the shipping companies in Shanghai have agreed that starting from September 16, passenger and freight fares will be paid in cash, and at most 10-day promissory notes will no longer be recorded. This newspaper once recorded this matter. However, after this announcement, all customs brokers unanimously opposed it and refused to pay in cash. In the past few days, the shipping companies and customs brokers have been negotiating on this matter. According to the customs brokers' requirement for 45-day payment period, the shipping companies have agreed to make concessions after public discussions and changed it to 25-day payment period. It is still under discussion and will probably be decided in a month.

The Completion of the Dongtang Project the Pond Works Association Entertained People from All Walks of Life Yesterday 135

Shen Yi, Mu Ouchu, and Others Gave Speeches in Succession

The Traffic at Gaogiao Breaks the Silence

The Jiangnan Seawall had been in disrepair for many years, and in last year's autumn flood season, it was almost in danger. Fortunately, it was rescued properly and nothing happened. Subsequently, under the supervision and assistance of the government and the people, the Jiangnan Pond Works Committee proceeded smoothly and has completed its work. The Association entertained people from all walks of life yesterday afternoon to visit the Gaogiao Pond Works in Pudong. At around 2:00 pm, they arrived at the seawall to inspect the various sections, accounting for seven or eight tenths of the entire Gaogiao project. Due to limited funds, it can only be safely maintained for a while and is not very solid. The details are recorded as follows:

Departing Personnel: Yesterday at 1:00 pm, the visitors from all walks of life gathered at the Bund Bronze Man Wharf and immediately boarded a ship to depart. The Jiangnan Pond Works Committee was led by Vice Chairman Mu Ouchu, Committee Members Jin Houcheng, Xu Guanzhi, Tang Chengzong, Zhong Renjie, Shi Wendan, and Director of the Municipal Government Works Bureau Shen Yi, etc. They arrived at Gaogiao around 2:00 pm and disembarked, then took a car to the car station, and then hired rickshaws to go to the Pond Works Office for inspection.

Overview of Dongtang: Dongtang is 16 kilometers long. The old seawall protection project was incomplete, which led to a sudden danger on August 24 last year when it encountered a hurricane. At that time, there were more than ten places that were urgently repaired. The construction of the current project is limited by funds and can only be built in the most important places, which is not even seven tenths of the dangerous places last year. A total of nine sections were built this year, including seven sections of stone work and two sections of cement work, with a total length of more than 2 kilometers and a total project cost of more than 284,000 yuan. Construction started successively on June 20, and it has been more than two months now. Except for the Yuanyi cement work section, which has not been completed due to changes in the plan, the remaining eight sections have all been completed. The old-style stone work is used, but the stone is replaced with 1-3-6 concrete cement glue. The wood is also slightly lengthened. Due to the different structures, there are three types: two stones, three stones, and three barrages. There are seven locations for this project. According to the terrain, tide, and wind and wave conditions, separate plans are made for the required work. Except for the large stones purchased by the Works Bureau itself, the rest are contracted by the Zhongnan Company. A total of more than 11,540 cubic meters of large stones are used, costing more than 45,830 yuan. The remaining labor and materials are contracted for more than 159,900 yuan, totaling 205,759 yuan and 61 cents. The cement work was built before the Works Bureau took over. After last year's unusual storm, a section of the Yuanyi section's wall collapsed, and the cement wall of the Rongzi section also tilted outward. This time, it is a repair work and an additional protection wall project. All the required labor and materials are contracted by the Zhongnan Company, costing 74,756 yuan. Because of the change in plan, the collapsed wall of the Yuanyi section has been purchased 997 cubic meters of large stones by the Works Bureau for a supply of 3,887 yuan, totaling 78,643 yuan.

Shen and Mu's Speeches: After inspecting the various places, there are the Shuizi section, Yizi section, Yuanzi section, Qiangzi section, Rongzi section, Juzi section, and Chenfu section. As for the Shouzi and Yuzi sections, they were not visited due to time constraints. After the visit, at 5:00 pm, Zhang Danru, director of the Pudong Pond Works Management Office, entertained people from all walks of life to rest at the Pond Works Office. Director Shen then reported that this pond work started on June 15 and was completed in mid-September, which took about three months. Thanks to the success of local people and the Pond Works Committee, Vice Chairman Mu, etc. Subsequently, Mr. Mu reported that the pond work repair funds were 150,000 from the municipal government, 400,000 from the provincial government, 250,000 from the Ministry of Railways, and 10,000 from the flood relief donation, totaling 810,000, which can only treat the symptoms. If it is to treat the root cause, it will cost millions, so the completion of this project can be said to be a very small part of treating the symptoms, and at most it can be safely maintained for half a year. The danger is still inevitable. I hope that the National Government can extract millions of yuan from the absence of a way to fundamentally repair it, so that it can be done once and for all. At around 6:00 pm, they boarded a ship and returned.

Northeast Puppet Advisor, American Kinney, Transfers from Shanghai to Geneva 139

According to the China East News Agency, the Northeast puppet government, intending to probe the intentions of various countries, has specially dispatched two American puppet advisors to Geneva to assist the Japanese delegation in attending the current session of the League of Nations General Assembly. One of the individuals from the puppet government arrived in Shanghai the night before last and is scheduled to depart Shanghai for Europe on the 27th of this month. A reporter from the China East News Agency went to interview him, as this is the first time since the establishment of the Northeast puppet government that such a puppet figure from the puppet government has been discovered on the maritime front.

Circumstances of Departure: It has been learned that the puppet government has dispatched a total of two puppet advisors to Geneva, both of whom are American. The one who arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday is named Kinney. He used to work for the Northeast Railway Bureau, and his behavior and thinking have always been pro-Japanese, so it is not surprising that he has joined the puppet government. As for the other person, named Brabson, he used to be a consultant to the National Government, enjoying his salary while occasionally engaging in foreign propaganda for us. After the establishment of the puppet government, he was recruited by the Japanese, and he willingly became a tool of the Japanese and devoted himself to propaganda against our country. With the opening of the current League of Nations General Assembly, the puppet government has sent these two individuals to Geneva in order to probe the intentions of various countries.

Separate Departures: The puppet government has already decided to send the two individuals, but there was no suitable task assigned to them. It was then decided to order the two to participate in the work of the Japanese delegation to the League of Nations. After receiving the order, Brabson left first. His current whereabouts should already be in America. As for Kinney, he was scheduled to travel from Changchun to Harbin on September 11th, and then transfer via the Siberian Railway to Europe. With his itinerary set, Kinney, along with Mr. Pan Lingdun, a reporter stationed in Changchun for the London Daily Mail, set off from Changchun on that day in the afternoon.

Ambush on the Way: Kinney and Pan Lingdun set off from Changchun, knowing that the anti-Japanese volunteer army along the way was very powerful. For safety, they dispatched many Japanese soldiers to escort the train. Unexpectedly, at 10:30 PM that night, when the train arrived at Yaomen, the tracks there were suddenly sabotaged by the volunteer army, and the train derailed. At that time, the train was brightly lit, while the outside was extremely dark. The volunteer army took advantage of this natural assistance and immediately shot and killed the Japanese soldiers in the train from the dark. They then boarded the train to search. Kinney, at this time, also tried to escape. He found a burlap sack on the way and used it to cover himself, walking on foot to Harbin. His original plan to go to Europe via Siberia was changed due to fear of the volunteer army's strength. He changed his plan to go from Harbin to Dalian, and from Dalian, he took a ship to Shanghai.

Puppet's Talk: This puppet advisor under the puppet government arrived in Shanghai on a Japanese ship, the Fengtian Maru, from Dalian the day before yesterday afternoon. According to what he told the reporter, he will stay in Shanghai for three days and then leave Shanghai on the 27th of this month on the Japanese ship Saww Maru for Europe. He also talked about the experience of being ambushed by the volunteer army on the way, saying that on the afternoon of September 11th, he and his friend Pan Lingdun traveled from Changchun to Harbin. At 10:30 PM that night, after two-thirds of the journey had been completed, the tracks were suddenly sabotaged by the volunteer army near Yaomen, and the entire train was surrounded. All the Japanese soldiers on the train were killed. His compartment was shot at more than fifty times, but fortunately, he lay down and was not injured at first. When the volunteer army boarded the train to search, he jumped off, lay in a ditch, and then jumped into the sorghum fields. After the volunteer army retreated, he found a military uniform left by the volunteer army, covered himself, and escaped.

Heilongjiang Province Suffers Even More, Turning into a Vast Swamp

According to the flood investigation report from Jilin and Heilongjiang provinces, there are over 40,000 flood victims in Yilan County, Jilin Province, with a shortage of food. Preparations for the Municipal National Goods Exhibition 142

The Shanghai Municipal National Goods Exhibition has been decided to be held at the Penglai Market on October 10th, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now heard that there are three main sections: internal display and exhibition, temporary market, and recreational activities. The general public believes that this is a good way to promote national goods and to seek sales for various national goods manufacturers. The exhibits in the internal display section can be freely retrieved by the manufacturers from the date of the exhibition's closing. The temporary market will be arranged by the organizers with electricity and running water, and participating merchants will select their own responsible persons to compete for sales on site. The recreational activities section will feature voluntary performances of songs and dances by outstanding experts from reputable girls' schools. The spoken drama section will be voluntarily participated in by reputable playwrights. An advertising section will be added, and a special publication will be printed for the publicity of various manufacturers. Manufacturers who wish to display exhibits or participate in the temporary market are welcome. The recreational activities section will not charge admission fees. Anyone who purchases national goods at the venue will be entitled to a voucher for the recreational activities section. The recreational activities section can use the voucher to welcome visitors to the venue. This promotion of national goods is funded by a special appropriation from the municipal government, purely for the benefit of the national goods manufacturers themselves and to cultivate the public's psychology and habit of loving and using national goods, mutually encouraging and praising the spirit of national independence. Chairman Lin of the National Government pays extreme attention and has specially inscribed the words "Enriching the Country and Benefiting the People." On the opening day, Mayor Wu will invite various agencies and organizations to participate in the ceremony. It is truly an unprecedented exhibition. In recent days, various manufacturers have been rushing to register for the sake of the honor of their own products.

Second Meeting of the National Goods Promotion Association 143

Eleven Additional Members, Including Wang Yansong, Appointed as Committee Members

The National Goods Promotion Committee of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce convened its second committee meeting yesterday (the 24th) at 2 PM. Fang Jiaobo chaired the meeting, and Wu Jichun served as the recorder. After the usual formalities, the minutes of the first meeting were read, followed by the report on matters: (A) The organizational outline of the association and the regulations of the branch associations, which were approved at the previous meeting, have been approved by the standing committee for record-keeping. (B) Director Chen Songyuan firmly requested to resign. After unsuccessful attempts to retain him, the standing committee decided to appoint Fang Jiaobo as the director. (C) The original number of committee members of the association had not yet been determined according to the regulations. Now, after the fourth executive committee meeting, it was decided to add eleven people, including Wang Yansong and Luo Qinghua, as committee members, totaling twenty-eight people. Post-War Reconstruction Funds for this City 144

Distribution Plan for 270,000 Dollars Determined

The Zhabei, Wusong, Wan, Yinhang, Pengpu, Yinxiang, and Zhenru districts of this city have suffered enormous losses since the war. The municipal government, in order to plan for the restoration of normalcy in the Wusong and other districts, had requested the National Government's Shanghai War Zone Reconstruction Committee to allocate funds for relief. The committee has approved an allocation of 250,000 dollars to be distributed by the Municipal War Zone Reconstruction Committee. This was brought up for discussion at the 11th meeting on the 22nd and the following decisions were made:

Distribution Plan: (1) Petty loans for the poor: 45,000 dollars. (2) Housing construction loans: 123,000 dollars. (The above two items will have 20,000 dollars withdrawn to be used as relief funds for secondary schools in the city affected by the disaster.) (3) Small industry loans: 40,000 dollars. These loans will be handled by the Social Affairs Bureau's General Loan Office and are specifically for small industries affected by the war and unable to continue operating, with loans of up to 500 dollars. The lending procedures will be determined separately. (4) Charitable organization housing and equipment repair loans: 25,000 dollars. Charitable organizations in the war zone, such as the Second Vagrant Rehabilitation Center and the Chinese Women and Children Relief Association, have been destroyed and have no funds to repair them. In order to ensure the continuation of charitable activities, this loan is specially set up to meet the needs. The number is not temporarily limited and will be determined after reviewing the needs of the requesting organizations. It will be handled by the Social Affairs Bureau's General Loan Office, and the procedures will be determined separately. (5) Zhabei porridge distribution expenses: 10,000 dollars. (6) General Loan Office start-up expenses: 7,000 dollars. The General Loan Office's regular expenses are not included. The equipment expenses for the General Loan Office are 505 dollars, and the equipment expenses for the seven branch loan offices are 1,050 dollars. The estimated printing expenses for two years are 5,044.46 dollars. (7) Relief funds for secondary schools in the city affected by the disaster: 40,000 dollars. The total of the above seven items is 270,000 dollars. In addition to the 250,000 dollars allocated by the Shanghai War Zone Reconstruction Committee, the remaining 20,000 dollars will be raised by the Municipal War Zone Reconstruction Committee itself.

Installment Payments: The above seven items, except for items 5, 6, and 7, which will be paid in full in the first installment, will be paid in two installments. The first installment includes: petty loans for the poor: 18,000 dollars, housing construction loans: 73,000 dollars, small industry loans: 19,500 dollars, charitable organization repair loans: 25,000 dollars, Zhabei porridge distribution expenses: 7,500 dollars, General Loan Office start-up expenses: 7,000 dollars, and relief funds for secondary schools affected by the disaster: 40,000 dollars, totaling 170,000 dollars. The second installment includes: petty loans for the poor: 27,000 dollars, housing construction loans: 50,000 dollars, small industry loans: 20,500 dollars, and Zhabei porridge distribution expenses: 2,500 dollars, totaling 100,000 dollars. The total of the two installments is 270,000 dollars.

Verdict in the San You She Labor-Capital Lawsuit Announced 145

Original Lawsuit and Counter-Lawsuit Both Dismissed, Litigation Costs Borne Separately

General Labor Union Committee Visits Mayor to Request Prompt Handling

The factory shutdown dispute at the San You Industrial Society in Yinxiang Port, Hudong, was arbitrated by the Municipal Government's Arbitration Committee. The labor side expressed that they would accept it with pain, while the capital side declared their objection and filed a lawsuit with the local court, requesting three points: (1) That the 20th arbitration decision made by the Shanghai Labor-Capital Arbitration Committee on September 1st of this year be abolished. (2) That it be confirmed that the original workers of the San You Industrial Society's Yinxiang Port factory have already been dismissed, and that the defendant hand over the occupied parts of the factory and equipment to the original plaintiff for acceptance. (3) That the litigation costs be borne by the defendant. The court hearing was held on the 21st of this month, and both parties hired lawyers to appear in court for defense. The labor side also filed a counter-lawsuit, requesting compensation for losses during the shutdown period. The presiding judge announced that the verdict would be announced on the 24th (i.e., yesterday). Yesterday afternoon at 3 PM, Gong Yuting and Zhang Youhai, the legal representatives of the 7th District Cotton Weaving Industry Union, along with more than ten workers who had attended the hearing, appeared in court at 10 AM to await the verdict. The plaintiff did not send anyone to the court. Judge Zhao Shulan, Judges Wang Run and Wang Shicheng, along with the clerk, took their seats in the Sixth Civil Court and announced the verdict: the plaintiff's lawsuit and the defendant's counter-lawsuit were both dismissed, and the litigation costs were to be borne separately. The written statement of reasons will be delivered to both parties within three days.

Furthermore, the Shanghai General Labor Union, due to the capital side of the San You factory not complying with the arbitration and defying the orders of the Party and government agencies by refusing to pay the workers' food allowances, which have been unpaid for four periods, resulting in the entire workforce facing starvation and in an extremely critical situation, members of the union, Zhu Xuefan, Shao Xubai, Zhou Xuexiang, Ye Xianggao, and Zhao Zhenyao, together with Xia Zhongzhao and Bao Boyi, representatives of the 7th District Cotton Workers Union, visited Mayor Wu at the Municipal Government at 10 AM yesterday. Mayor Wu personally received them. The representatives stated their intentions, saying that although the capital side's defiance of the arbitration decision by filing a lawsuit in court was scheduled to be decided today (i.e., yesterday), it was difficult to determine when it would be resolved. The prolongation of the dispute was causing great anxiety, and the capital side had also taken the opportunity to stop paying food allowances, causing the workers to face the fear of starvation. If a prompt solution was not found, it would lead to unfortunate incidents, so they asked the mayor to pay attention to it. Mayor Wu replied that the municipal government was waiting for the court's verdict on the San You case, and after the court's verdict, the municipal government would strictly enforce it. As for the capital side's suspension of workers' food allowances, the municipal government also had a solution and would definitely not allow the workers to starve. The representatives were satisfied and left.
